</a>    <a href="/xuesongbj/Rust-Notes/blob/86150f2a85a36cf1d06e3de9817b1663d86aa788/Rust%E5%AD%A6%E4%B9%A0%E7%AC%94%E8%AE%B0_%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80/%E9%94%99%E8%AF%AF/%E5%8F%AF%E6%81%A2%E5%A4%8D%E9%94%99%E8%AF%AF.md" data-permalink-href="/xuesongbj/Rust-Notes/blob/86150f2a85a36cf1d06e3de9817b1663d86aa788/Rust%E5%AD%A6%E4%B9%A0%E7%AC%94%E8%AE%B0_%E5%9F%BA%E7%A1%80/%E9%94%99%E8%AF%AF/%E5%8F%AF%E6%81%A2%E5%A4%8D%E9%94%99%E8%AF%AF.md" aria-label="Display the rendered blob" data-view-component="true" class="rendered tooltipped tooltipped tooltipped-n selected js-permalink-replaceable-link btn-sm btn BtnGroup-item">  <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-file">
    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M3.75 1.5a.25.25 0 00-.25.25v11.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h8.5a.25.25 0 00.25-.25V6H9.75A1.75 1.75 0 018 4.25V1.5H3.75zm5.75.56v2.19c0 .138.112.25.25.25h2.19L9.5 2.06zM2 1.75C2 .784 2.784 0 3.75 0h5.086c.464 0 .909.184 1.237.513l3.414 3.414c.329.328.513.773.513 1.237v8.086A1.75 1.75 0 0112.25 15h-8.5A1.75 1.75 0 012 13.25V1.75z"></path>
</svg>
</a>  </div>

        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-可恢复错误" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#可恢复错误"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>可恢复错误</h1>
<p dir="auto">可恢复性（recoverable）错误通常指一种状态，比如打开文件时，没找到，应该新建。显然，最终如何处理，由调用方负责。没有异常，对于可恢复性错误，返回<code>Result&lt;T, E&gt;</code>对象。</p>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-option" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#option"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Option</h2>
<p dir="auto">Rust中没有 <code>null</code> 值的概念，在Rust中，可能失败并希望指示缺失相应值的API会返回 <code>Option</code>。当任何API及其后续值想要表示缺少值时，此错误类型就是合适的。简而言之，它与<code>null</code>值类似，不过这里的 <code>null</code> 值检查是显式的，并且在编译期由类型系统强制执行。</p>
<p dir="auto">Option包含以下标签签名:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pub enum Option&lt;T&gt; {
    /// 没有值
    None,

    /// 包含某些值 'T'
    Some(T),
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">pub</span> <span class="pl-k">enum</span> <span class="pl-en">Option</span>&lt;T&gt; {
    <span class="pl-c">/// 没有值</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">None</span>,

    <span class="pl-c">/// 包含某些值 'T'</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">Some</span>(T),
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<p dir="auto">它是包含两个变体的枚举，并且 <code>T</code> 是泛型。操作成功时，可以使用Some(T)存储任意类型值<code>T</code>，或者使用 <code>None</code> 变量表示操作失败的情况下该值为null。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="let wrapped_i32 = Some(2);          // Some(T)

let empty: Option&lt;i32&gt; = None;      // None

let empty = None::&lt;i32&gt;;            // None"><pre><span class="pl-k">let</span> wrapped_i32 <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Some</span>(<span class="pl-c1">2</span>);          <span class="pl-c">// Some(T)</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> empty: <span class="pl-k">Option</span><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-k">i32</span><span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>;      <span class="pl-c">// None</span>

<span class="pl-k">let</span> empty <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-k">i32</span><span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>;            <span class="pl-c">// None</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-prelude模块" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#prelude模块"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>prelude模块</h3>
<p dir="auto">Rust的标准库，有一个 <code>prelude</code> 子模块，该模块自动导入了常用的类型、函数和任意标准库模块的重新导出。导入后，允许直接通过变体实例话 <code>Option</code> 值。</p>
<p dir="auto">目前版本导入以下内容:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="//! [mem::drop]: crate::mem::drop
//! [std::borrow]: crate::borrow
//! [std::boxed]: crate::boxed
//! [std::clone]: crate::clone
//! [std::cmp]: crate::cmp
//! [std::convert]: crate::convert
//! [std::default]: crate::default
//! [std::iter]: crate::iter
//! [std::marker]: crate::marker
//! [std::mem]: crate::mem
//! [std::ops]: crate::ops
//! [std::option]: crate::option
//! [`std::prelude::v1`]: v1
//! [std::result]: crate::result
//! [std::slice]: crate::slice
//! [std::string]: crate::string
//! [std::vec]: mod@crate::vec
//! [`to_owned`]: crate::borrow::ToOwned::to_owned
//! [book-closures]: ../../book/ch13-01-closures.html
//! [book-dtor]: ../../book/ch15-03-drop.html
//! [book-enums]: ../../book/ch06-01-defining-an-enum.html
//! [book-iter]: ../../book/ch13-02-iterators.html"><pre><span class="pl-c">//! [mem::drop]: crate::mem::drop</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::borrow]: crate::borrow</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::boxed]: crate::boxed</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::clone]: crate::clone</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::cmp]: crate::cmp</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::convert]: crate::convert</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::default]: crate::default</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::iter]: crate::iter</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::marker]: crate::marker</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::mem]: crate::mem</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::ops]: crate::ops</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::option]: crate::option</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [`std::prelude::v1`]: v1</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::result]: crate::result</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::slice]: crate::slice</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::string]: crate::string</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [std::vec]: mod@crate::vec</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [`to_owned`]: crate::borrow::ToOwned::to_owned</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [book-closures]: ../../book/ch13-01-closures.html</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [book-dtor]: ../../book/ch15-03-drop.html</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [book-enums]: ../../book/ch06-01-defining-an-enum.html</span>
<span class="pl-c">//! [book-iter]: ../../book/ch13-02-iterators.html</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-option-交互" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#option-交互"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Option 交互</h3>
<p dir="auto">如下实例，<code>value</code> 是一个 <code>Option&lt;&amp;i32&gt;</code>。<code>get()</code> 方法返回的是一个 <code>Option&lt;&amp;i32&gt;</code>，而不是其内部的值(<code>&amp;i32</code>)。为了给 <code>value</code>的值加1，我们需要从 <code>Option</code>中提取 <code>i32</code>。为了检查变体，我们有两种方法，他们分别是 <code>模式匹配</code> 和 <code>if let</code> 语句。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="use std::collections::HashMap;

fn main() {
    let mut map = HashMap::new();
    map.insert(&quot;one&quot;, 1);
    map.insert(&quot;two&quot;, 2);

    let incremented_value = match map.get(&quot;one&quot;) {
        Some(val) =&gt; val + 1,
        None =&gt; 0
    };

    println!(&quot;{}&quot;, incremented_value);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">use</span> std<span class="pl-k">::</span>collections<span class="pl-k">::</span>HashMap;

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-k">mut</span> map <span class="pl-k">=</span> HashMap<span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">new</span>();
    map.<span class="pl-en">insert</span>(<span class="pl-s">"one"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
    map.<span class="pl-en">insert</span>(<span class="pl-s">"two"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>);

    <span class="pl-k">let</span> incremented_value <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">match</span> map.<span class="pl-en">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"one"</span>) {
        <span class="pl-c1">Some</span>(val) <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> val <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>,
        <span class="pl-c1">None</span> <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    };

    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"{}"</span>, incremented_value);
}</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="use std::collections::HashMap;

fn main() {
    let mut map = HashMap::new();
    map.insert(&quot;one&quot;, 1);
    map.insert(&quot;two&quot;, 2);

    let incremented_value = if let Some(v) = map.get(&quot;one&quot;) {
        v + 1
    } else {
        0
    };

    println!(&quot;{}&quot;, incremented_value);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">use</span> std<span class="pl-k">::</span>collections<span class="pl-k">::</span>HashMap;

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-k">mut</span> map <span class="pl-k">=</span> HashMap<span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">new</span>();
    map.<span class="pl-en">insert</span>(<span class="pl-s">"one"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
    map.<span class="pl-en">insert</span>(<span class="pl-s">"two"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>);

    <span class="pl-k">let</span> incremented_value <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-c1">Some</span>(v) <span class="pl-k">=</span> map.<span class="pl-en">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"one"</span>) {
        v <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>
    } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
        <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
    };

    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"{}"</span>, incremented_value);
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">当我们对值的某个变体感兴趣并希望对其他变体进行常规的操作时，推荐使用这种方法。<code>if let</code> 语句表述更简洁。</p>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-unwrapping" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#unwrapping"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Unwrapping</h3>
<p dir="auto"><code>Result&lt;T, E&gt;</code> 类型定义了很多辅助方法来处理各种情况，其中之一叫做<code>unwrap</code>。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>如果<code>Result</code>值是成员<code>OK</code>, <code>unwrap</code>会返回<code>OK</code>中的值。</li>
<li>如果<code>Result</code>是成员<code>Err</code>，<code>unwrap</code>会为我们调用<code>panic!</code>。</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Unwrapping是一种不太安全的方法在 <code>Option</code> 上调用解压缩方法。如果返回的结果是 <code>Some</code>，那么调用 <code>unwrap()</code> 和 <code>expect()</code>方法提取内部的值；如果返回的结果是 <code>None</code>，则会发生异常。</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>仅当我们确定 <code>Option</code> 值确实包含某个值时，才推荐使用这些方法。</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="use std::collections::HashMap;

fn main() {
    let mut map = HashMap::new();
    map.insert(&quot;one&quot;, 1);
    map.insert(&quot;two&quot;, 2);

    let incremented_value = map.get(&quot;two&quot;).unwrap() + 1;
    println!(&quot;{}&quot;, incremented_value);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">use</span> std<span class="pl-k">::</span>collections<span class="pl-k">::</span>HashMap;

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-k">mut</span> map <span class="pl-k">=</span> HashMap<span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">new</span>();
    map.<span class="pl-en">insert</span>(<span class="pl-s">"one"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
    map.<span class="pl-en">insert</span>(<span class="pl-s">"two"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>);

    <span class="pl-k">let</span> incremented_value <span class="pl-k">=</span> map.<span class="pl-en">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"two"</span>).<span class="pl-en">unwrap</span>() <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"{}"</span>, incremented_value);
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>get</code>一个不存在的<strong>键值</strong>，则发生异常。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="use std::collections::HashMap;

fn main() {
    let mut map = HashMap::new();
    map.insert(&quot;one&quot;, 1);
    map.insert(&quot;two&quot;, 2);

    let incremented_value = map.get(&quot;three&quot;).unwrap() + 1;
    println!(&quot;{}&quot;, incremented_value);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">use</span> std<span class="pl-k">::</span>collections<span class="pl-k">::</span>HashMap;

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-k">mut</span> map <span class="pl-k">=</span> HashMap<span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">new</span>();
    map.<span class="pl-en">insert</span>(<span class="pl-s">"one"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
    map.<span class="pl-en">insert</span>(<span class="pl-s">"two"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>);

    <span class="pl-k">let</span> incremented_value <span class="pl-k">=</span> map.<span class="pl-en">get</span>(<span class="pl-s">"three"</span>).<span class="pl-en">unwrap</span>() <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>;
    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"{}"</span>, incremented_value);
}</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="root@8d75790f92f5:~/rs/ddd/src# cargo r
   Compiling ddd v0.1.0 (/root/rs/ddd)
    Finished dev [unoptimized + debuginfo] target(s) in 5.21s
     Running `/root/rs/ddd/target/debug/ddd`
thread 'main' panicked at 'called `Option::unwrap()` on a `None` value', src/main.rs:12:46
note: run with `RUST_BACKTRACE=1` environment variable to display a backtrace"><pre>root@8d75790f92f5:~<span class="pl-k">/</span>rs<span class="pl-k">/</span>ddd<span class="pl-k">/</span>src# cargo r
   Compiling ddd v0.<span class="pl-c1">1.0</span> (<span class="pl-k">/</span>root<span class="pl-k">/</span>rs<span class="pl-k">/</span>ddd)
    Finished dev [unoptimized <span class="pl-k">+</span> debuginfo] <span class="pl-en">target</span>(s) <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">5</span>.21s
     Running `<span class="pl-k">/</span>root<span class="pl-k">/</span>rs<span class="pl-k">/</span>ddd<span class="pl-k">/</span>target<span class="pl-k">/</span>debug<span class="pl-k">/</span>ddd`
thread <span class="pl-k">'<span class="pl-en">main</span></span>' panicked at <span class="pl-k">'<span class="pl-en">called</span></span> `<span class="pl-k">Option</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">unwrap</span>()` on a `<span class="pl-c1">None</span>` value', src<span class="pl-k">/</span>main.rs:<span class="pl-c1">12</span>:<span class="pl-c1">46</span>
note: run with `RUST_BACKTRACE<span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>` environment variable to display a backtrace</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h4 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-unwrap-和-expect-区别" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#unwrap-和-expect-区别"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>unwrap() 和 expect() 区别</h4>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>expect()</code> 是首选方法，因为它允许你传递一个字符串作为发生异常时输出的提示信息，同时显示源文件发生异常时的确切代码行号。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>unwrap()</code> 不允许你将调试信息作为参数进行传递，并显示在标准库源文件中 <code>Option</code> 下定义 <code>unwrap()</code>的代码行号。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-resultt-e" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#resultt-e"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Result&lt;T, E&gt;</h2>
<p dir="auto"><code>Result</code> 和 <code>Option</code> 类似，但具有一些优点，即能够存储和错误上下文有关的异常值，而不只是 <code>None</code>。<strong>当我们希望知道操作失败的原因时，此类型是合适的。</strong></p>
<p dir="auto"><code>Result</code>类型签名:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="enum Result&lt;T, E&gt; {
    Ok(T),
    Err(E),
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">enum</span> <span class="pl-en">Result</span>&lt;T, E&gt; {
    <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(T),
    <span class="pl-c1">Err</span>(E),
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<p dir="auto">它包含两个变体，并且都是泛型。<code>Ok(T)</code>是用于表示成功状态时放入任意值 <code>T</code> 的变体，而 <code>Err(E)</code> 是用于表示执行失败时放入任何异常值 <code>T</code>的变体。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fn main() {
    // Ok(T)
    let _my_result: Result&lt;_, ()&gt; = Ok(64);
    let _my_result = Ok::&lt;_, ()&gt;(64);

    // Err(E)
    let _my_err = Err::&lt;(), f32&gt;(354.3);
    let _other_err: Result&lt;bool, String&gt; = Err(&quot;Wait, What ?&quot;.to_string());
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-c">// Ok(T)</span>
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> _my_result: <span class="pl-k">Result</span><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>_, ()<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(<span class="pl-c1">64</span>);
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> _my_result <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>_, ()<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>(<span class="pl-c1">64</span>);

    <span class="pl-c">// Err(E)</span>
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> _my_err <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Err</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>(), <span class="pl-k">f32</span><span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>(<span class="pl-c1">354.3</span>);
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> _other_err: <span class="pl-k">Result</span><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-k">bool</span>, <span class="pl-k">String</span><span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Err</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Wait, What ?"</span>.<span class="pl-en">to_string</span>());
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">使用 <code>()</code> 指定 <code>Err</code> 变体的类型 <code>E</code>。可以使用 <code>_</code>来要求Rust为我们推断具体的类型。</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-result实例" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#result实例"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Result实例</h3>
<p dir="auto">标准库中的许多文件操作API都会返回 <code>Result</code> 类型，因为可能存在不同的操作失败原因，例如找不到文件(file not found)、目录不存在(directory does not exists)，以及权限错误(permission errors)等。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="use std::fs::File;
use std::io::Read;
use std::path::Path;

fn main() {
    let path = Path::new(&quot;data.txt&quot;);
    let mut file = match File::open(&amp;path) {
        Ok(file)    =&gt; file,
        Err(err)    =&gt; panic!(&quot;Error while opening file: {}&quot;, err),
    };

    let mut s = String::new();
    let _ = file.read_to_string(&amp;mut s);
    println!(&quot;Message: {}&quot;, s);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">use</span> std<span class="pl-k">::</span>fs<span class="pl-k">::</span>File;
<span class="pl-k">use</span> std<span class="pl-k">::</span>io<span class="pl-k">::</span>Read;
<span class="pl-k">use</span> std<span class="pl-k">::</span>path<span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-k">Path</span>;

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> path <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">Path</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">new</span>(<span class="pl-s">"data.txt"</span>);
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-k">mut</span> file <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">match</span> File<span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">open</span>(<span class="pl-k">&amp;</span>path) {
        <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(file)    <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> file,
        <span class="pl-c1">Err</span>(err)    <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">panic!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Error while opening file: {}"</span>, err),
    };

    <span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-k">mut</span> s <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">String</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">new</span>();
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> _ <span class="pl-k">=</span> file.<span class="pl-en">read_to_string</span>(<span class="pl-k">&amp;</span><span class="pl-k">mut</span> s);
    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Message: {}"</span>, s);
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-传播" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#传播"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>传播</h3>
<p dir="auto">可通过 <code>return Err</code>将错误按调用堆栈传递出去。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fn div(x: i32, y: i32) -&gt; Result&lt;i32, &amp;'static str&gt; {
    if y != 0 { 
        Ok(x / y) 
    } else { 
        Err(&quot;divide by zero&quot;) 
    }
}

fn test(x: i32, y: i32) -&gt; Result&lt;i32, &amp;'static str&gt; {
    let z = div(x, y);
    if z.is_err() { return z; }  // 传播！
    z
}

fn main() {
    test(3, 0).unwrap();        // 处理错误！
}                                      "><pre><span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">div</span>(x: <span class="pl-k">i32</span>, y: <span class="pl-k">i32</span>) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">Result</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">i32</span>, &amp;<span class="pl-k">'<span class="pl-en">static</span></span> <span class="pl-k">str</span>&gt; {
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> y <span class="pl-k">!=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> { 
        <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(x <span class="pl-k">/</span> y) 
    } <span class="pl-k">else</span> { 
        <span class="pl-c1">Err</span>(<span class="pl-s">"divide by zero"</span>) 
    }
}

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">test</span>(x: <span class="pl-k">i32</span>, y: <span class="pl-k">i32</span>) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">Result</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">i32</span>, &amp;<span class="pl-k">'<span class="pl-en">static</span></span> <span class="pl-k">str</span>&gt; {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> z <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">div</span>(x, y);
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> z.<span class="pl-en">is_err</span>() { <span class="pl-k">return</span> z; }  <span class="pl-c">// 传播！</span>
    z
}

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-en">test</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>).<span class="pl-en">unwrap</span>();        <span class="pl-c">// 处理错误！</span>
}                                      </pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="root@8d75790f92f5:~/rs/ddd/src# cargo r
   Compiling ddd v0.1.0 (/root/rs/ddd)
    Finished dev [unoptimized + debuginfo] target(s) in 3.55s
     Running `/root/rs/ddd/target/debug/ddd`
thread 'main' panicked at 'called `Result::unwrap()` on an `Err` value: &quot;divide by zero&quot;', src/main.rs:22:16
note: run with `RUST_BACKTRACE=1` environment variable to display a backtrace"><pre>root@8d75790f92f5:~<span class="pl-k">/</span>rs<span class="pl-k">/</span>ddd<span class="pl-k">/</span>src# cargo r
   Compiling ddd v0.<span class="pl-c1">1.0</span> (<span class="pl-k">/</span>root<span class="pl-k">/</span>rs<span class="pl-k">/</span>ddd)
    Finished dev [unoptimized <span class="pl-k">+</span> debuginfo] <span class="pl-en">target</span>(s) <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>.55s
     Running `<span class="pl-k">/</span>root<span class="pl-k">/</span>rs<span class="pl-k">/</span>ddd<span class="pl-k">/</span>target<span class="pl-k">/</span>debug<span class="pl-k">/</span>ddd`
thread <span class="pl-k">'<span class="pl-en">main</span></span>' panicked at <span class="pl-k">'<span class="pl-en">called</span></span> `<span class="pl-k">Result</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">unwrap</span>()` on an `<span class="pl-c1">Err</span>` value: <span class="pl-s">"divide by zero"</span>', src<span class="pl-k">/</span>main.rs:<span class="pl-c1">22</span>:<span class="pl-c1">16</span>
note: run with `RUST_BACKTRACE<span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>` environment variable to display a backtrace</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-optionresult的组合" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#optionresult的组合"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Option/Result的组合</h2>
<p dir="auto">由于 <code>Option</code> 和 <code>Result</code> 是包装器类型，因此安全地与其内部值进行交互的唯一方法是通过<strong>模式匹配</strong>或<strong>if let语句</strong>。这些包装器类型附带了很多辅助方法，这些被称为<strong>组合器</strong>，其上的实现允许用户轻松地操作内部值。</p>
<p dir="auto">这些是泛型方法，根据使用场景不同而包含多种，例如 <code>Ok(T)/Some(T)</code>，而其中一些方法用于处理失败的值，例如 <code>Err(E)/None</code>。某些方法用于拆解和提取内部值，而有些方法会保留包装器类型的结构，仅修改内部值。</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">注意:</p>
<p dir="auto">成功值时，通常指的是 <code>Ok(T)/Some(T)</code>变量；失败值时，通常指的是 <code>Err(T)/None(T)</code> 变量。</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-常见的组合器" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#常见的组合器"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>常见的组合器</h3>
<p dir="auto"><code>map()</code> 此方法允许你将表示成功的值 <code>T</code> 转换为另一个值 <code>U</code>。以下是 <code>Option</code> 类型对应 <code>map</code> 特征签名:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pub fn map&lt;U, F&gt;(self, f: F) -&gt; Option&lt;U&gt;
where
    F: FnOnce(T) -&gt; U
{
    match self {
        Some(x) =&gt; Some(f(x)),
        None =&gt; None,
    }
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">pub</span> <span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">map</span>&lt;U, F&gt;(<span class="pl-c1">self</span>, f: F) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">Option</span>&lt;U&gt;
<span class="pl-k">where</span>
    F: <span class="pl-c1">FnOnce</span>(T) -&gt; U
{
    <span class="pl-k">match</span> <span class="pl-c1">self</span> {
        <span class="pl-c1">Some</span>(x) <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">Some</span>(<span class="pl-en">f</span>(x)),
        <span class="pl-c1">None</span> <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>,
    }
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<p dir="auto">以下是和Result类型有关的签名:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="pub fn map&lt;U, F&gt;(self, f: F) -&gt; Option&lt;U&gt;
where F: FnOne(T) -&gt; U {
    match self {
        Ok(t) =&gt; Ok(f(t)),
        Err(e) =&gt; Err(e)
    }
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">pub</span> <span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">map</span>&lt;U, F&gt;(<span class="pl-c1">self</span>, f: F) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">Option</span>&lt;U&gt;
<span class="pl-k">where</span> F: FnOne(T) -&gt; U {
    <span class="pl-k">match</span> <span class="pl-c1">self</span> {
        <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(t) <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(<span class="pl-en">f</span>(t)),
        <span class="pl-c1">Err</span>(e) <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">Err</span>(e)
    }
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">这是特征的某种特殊类型，仅适用于闭包，因此具有 <code>(T) -&gt; U</code> 这样的函数签名。<code>FnOnce</code> 前缀表示此闭包取得输入参数 <code>T</code> 的所有权，并且我们只能用 <code>T</code> 调用此闭包一次，因为 <code>T</code> 将在执行调用后被使用。</p>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-组合器应用" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#组合器应用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>组合器应用</h3>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fn get_nth(items: &amp;Vec&lt;usize&gt;, nth: usize) -&gt; Option&lt;usize&gt; {
    if nth &lt; items.len() {
        Some(items[nth])
    } else {
        None
    }
}

fn double(val: usize) -&gt; usize {
    val * val
}

fn main() {
    let items = vec![7, 6, 5, 4, 3, 5, 3, 10, 3, 2, 4];
    println!(&quot;{}&quot;, items.len());

    let doubled = get_nth(&amp;items, 4).map(double);
    println!(&quot;{:?}&quot;, doubled);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">get_nth</span>(items: <span class="pl-k">&amp;</span><span class="pl-k">Vec</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">usize</span>&gt;, nth: <span class="pl-k">usize</span>) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">Option</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">usize</span>&gt; {
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> nth <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> items.<span class="pl-en">len</span>() {
        <span class="pl-c1">Some</span>(items[nth])
    } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
        <span class="pl-c1">None</span>
    }
}

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">double</span>(val: <span class="pl-k">usize</span>) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">usize</span> {
    val <span class="pl-k">*</span> val
}

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> items <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">vec!</span>[<span class="pl-c1">7</span>, <span class="pl-c1">6</span>, <span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">5</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">10</span>, <span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>];
    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"{}"</span>, items.<span class="pl-en">len</span>());

    <span class="pl-k">let</span> doubled <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">get_nth</span>(<span class="pl-k">&amp;</span>items, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>).<span class="pl-en">map</span>(double);
    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"{:?}"</span>, doubled);
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<p dir="auto">还可以提供一个内联形式的闭包，如下所示:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="let doubled = get_nth(&amp;items, 4).map(|v| v*v);"><pre><span class="pl-k">let</span> doubled <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">get_nth</span>(<span class="pl-k">&amp;</span>items, <span class="pl-c1">4</span>).<span class="pl-en">map</span>(<span class="pl-k">|</span>v<span class="pl-k">|</span> v<span class="pl-k">*</span>v);</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">这是链式调用的简易形式。并且比之前使用的 <code>match</code> 表达式和 <code>if let</code>语句更简单。</p>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-option-和-result-类型之间转换" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#option-和-result-类型之间转换"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Option 和 Result 类型之间转换</h2>
<p dir="auto">还有一些方法可以将一种包装器转换成另一种包装器类型。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ok_or</code>: 将 <code>Option</code>值转换为<code>Result</code>值，同时将错误值作为第二个参数进行接收。此类型的变体是<code>ok_or_else</code>方法，但优于此方法，因为它接收闭包来进行惰性求值。</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><code>ok</code>: 此方法将<code>Result</code>转化为调用<code>self</code>的Option，并且会丢弃<code>Err</code>值。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fn main() {
    let x = Some(&quot;foo&quot;);
    let _y = x.ok_or(0);
    assert_eq!(x.ok_or(0), Ok(&quot;foo&quot;));

    println!(&quot;xxx&quot;);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> x <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Some</span>(<span class="pl-s">"foo"</span>);
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> _y <span class="pl-k">=</span> x.<span class="pl-en">ok_or</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>);
    <span class="pl-c1">assert_eq!</span>(x.<span class="pl-en">ok_or</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span>), <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(<span class="pl-s">"foo"</span>));

    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"xxx"</span>);
}</pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="_y = core::result::Result&lt;&amp;str, i32&gt;::Ok(&quot;foo&quot;)
x = core::option::Option&lt;&amp;str&gt;::Some(&quot;foo&quot;)"><pre>_y <span class="pl-k">=</span> core<span class="pl-k">::</span>result<span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-k">Result</span><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-k">&amp;</span><span class="pl-k">str</span>, <span class="pl-k">i32</span><span class="pl-k">&gt;</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(<span class="pl-s">"foo"</span>)
x <span class="pl-k">=</span> core<span class="pl-k">::</span>option<span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-k">Option</span><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-k">&amp;</span><span class="pl-k">str</span><span class="pl-k">&gt;</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-c1">Some</span>(<span class="pl-s">"foo"</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-运算符-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#运算符-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>运算符 "?"</h2>
<p dir="auto">使用<code>?</code>来代替原来的<code>match</code>匹配的方式。<code>?</code>作用在函数的结束。</p>
<p dir="auto">它的运行机制如下: 当我们获得一个成功值时，希望立即提取它；当我们获得一个错误值时，希望提前返回，并将错误传播给调用方。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>要么解构出<code>Ok</code>关联值，要么<code>return Err</code>向外传播。</li>
<li>只能用在返回<code>Result&lt;T, E&gt;</code>或<code>Option</code>的函数中。</li>
<li>隐式传播的<code>Err</code>关键值类型必须相同，或可自动转换。</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="fn div(x: i32, y: i32) -&gt; Result&lt;i32, &amp;'static str&gt; {
    if y != 0 {
        Ok(x/ y)
    } else {
        Err(&quot;divide by zero&quot;)
    }
}

fn test(x: i32, y: i32) -&gt; Result&lt;i32, &amp;'static str&gt; {
    let z: i32 = div(x, y)?;            // z返回值为i32或者Err
                                        // 如果div函数结果正确，继续之后逻辑，直到程序结束

    Ok(z)                               // Ok将成功值，解构为Result进行返回
}

fn main() {
    test(3, 0).unwrap();
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">div</span>(x: <span class="pl-k">i32</span>, y: <span class="pl-k">i32</span>) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">Result</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">i32</span>, &amp;<span class="pl-k">'<span class="pl-en">static</span></span> <span class="pl-k">str</span>&gt; {
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> y <span class="pl-k">!=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span> {
        <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(x<span class="pl-k">/</span> y)
    } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
        <span class="pl-c1">Err</span>(<span class="pl-s">"divide by zero"</span>)
    }
}

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">test</span>(x: <span class="pl-k">i32</span>, y: <span class="pl-k">i32</span>) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">Result</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">i32</span>, &amp;<span class="pl-k">'<span class="pl-en">static</span></span> <span class="pl-k">str</span>&gt; {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> z: <span class="pl-k">i32</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">div</span>(x, y)?;            <span class="pl-c">// z返回值为i32或者Err</span>
                                        <span class="pl-c">// 如果div函数结果正确，继续之后逻辑，直到程序结束</span>

    <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(z)                               <span class="pl-c">// Ok将成功值，解构为Result进行返回</span>
}

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-en">test</span>(<span class="pl-c1">3</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>).<span class="pl-en">unwrap</span>();
}</pre></div>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-具体实例" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#具体实例"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>具体实例</h3>
<p dir="auto">它常用的 <code>match</code> 表达式来处理 <code>Result</code>类型:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="use std::string::FromUtf8Error;

fn str_upper_match(str: Vec&lt;u8&gt;) -&gt; Result&lt;String, FromUtf8Error&gt; {
    let ret = match String::from_utf8(str) {
        Ok(str) =&gt; str.to_uppercase(),
        Err(err) =&gt; return Err(err)
    };

    println!(&quot;Conversion succeeded: {}&quot;, ret);
    Ok(ret)
}

fn main() {
    let invalid_str = str_upper_match(vec![197, 198]);
    println!(&quot;{:?}&quot;, invalid_str);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">use</span> std<span class="pl-k">::</span>string<span class="pl-k">::</span>FromUtf8Error;

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">str_upper_match</span>(<span class="pl-k">str</span>: <span class="pl-k">Vec</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">u8</span>&gt;) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">Result</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">String</span>, FromUtf8Error&gt; {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> ret <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">match</span> <span class="pl-k">String</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">from_utf8</span>(<span class="pl-k">str</span>) {
        <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(<span class="pl-k">str</span>) <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">str</span>.<span class="pl-en">to_uppercase</span>(),
        <span class="pl-c1">Err</span>(err) <span class="pl-k">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">Err</span>(err)
    };

    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Conversion succeeded: {}"</span>, ret);
    <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(ret)
}

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> invalid_str <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">str_upper_match</span>(<span class="pl-c1">vec!</span>[<span class="pl-c1">197</span>, <span class="pl-c1">198</span>]);
    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"{:?}"</span>, invalid_str);
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">运算符 <code>?</code> 抽象了这种模式，这使我们能够以一种更简洁的方式编写 <code>bytes_to_str</code> 方法。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="use std::string::FromUtf8Error;

fn str_upper_concise(str: Vec&lt;u8&gt;) -&gt; Result&lt;String, FromUtf8Error&gt; {
    let ret = String::from_utf8(str).map(|s| s.to_uppercase())?;
    println!(&quot;Conversion succeeded: {}&quot;, ret);
    Ok(ret)
}

fn main() {
    let valid_str = str_upper_concise(vec![121, 97, 89]);
    println!(&quot;{:?}&quot;, valid_str);
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">use</span> std<span class="pl-k">::</span>string<span class="pl-k">::</span>FromUtf8Error;

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">str_upper_concise</span>(<span class="pl-k">str</span>: <span class="pl-k">Vec</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">u8</span>&gt;) -&gt; <span class="pl-k">Result</span>&lt;<span class="pl-k">String</span>, FromUtf8Error&gt; {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> ret <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">String</span><span class="pl-k">::</span><span class="pl-en">from_utf8</span>(<span class="pl-k">str</span>).<span class="pl-en">map</span>(<span class="pl-k">|</span>s<span class="pl-k">|</span> s.<span class="pl-en">to_uppercase</span>())?;
    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"Conversion succeeded: {}"</span>, ret);
    <span class="pl-c1">Ok</span>(ret)
}

<span class="pl-k">fn</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>() {
    <span class="pl-k">let</span> valid_str <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">str_upper_concise</span>(<span class="pl-c1">vec!</span>[<span class="pl-c1">121</span>, <span class="pl-c1">97</span>, <span class="pl-c1">89</span>]);
    <span class="pl-c1">println!</span>(<span class="pl-s">"{:?}"</span>, valid_str);
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"> </p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-链式调用" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#链式调用"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>链式调用</h3>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-rust position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="File.open(&quot;hello.txt&quot;)?.read_to_string(&amp;mut s)?;"><pre>File.<span class="pl-en">open</span>(<span class="pl-s">"hello.txt"</span>)?.<span class="pl-en">read_to_string</span>(<span class="pl-k">&amp;</span><span class="pl-k">mut</span> s)?;</pre></div>
</article>
  </div>
